# Text Elements
An attractive force is negative, When Radius -> inifnity, g-> 0
and as Radius increase, also increases g
hence g is negative, approaching to 0 as R increases ^aSDx1HPN

The work done per unit mass in bringing a Test mass, to bring an object
from infinity to a defined point ^H1l1lu5j

6x10^24 kg ^HX04mwgO

1.3x10^4km ^nTWxrDPV

6.4x10^3km ^u1J1sQtb

It is asking for the speed the pushed
the object to that height
Not the orbital Speed! ^vinLcOv4
